<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>гря́з<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, определительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> предикатив; неизменяемое. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — грязнее.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-гряз-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-н-о</b>.
</p>

***грязный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязный.html>гря́зный</a> (1187)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>грязь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grjazʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грязный.html>гря́зный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grjáznyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)грязне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)грязне́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">грязне́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dirty, soiled, dingy, filthy, grimy, grubby
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:грязный.html>гря́зные</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:сапог.html>сапоги́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">grjáznyje sapogí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dirty boots</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>dirty, low, vile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:грязный.html>гря́зная</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложь.html>ложь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">grjáznaja ložʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dirty lie</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>muddy</li>
<li>garbage, slop
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:грязный.html>гря́зное</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:ведро.html>ведро́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">grjáznoje vedró</i> ― <span class="e-translation">slop bucket</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>грязь</a> (1629)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*grę̑zь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>грязь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grjazʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mud</li>
<li>dirt (stain or spot (on clothes etc))</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> filth, smut, dirt</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:грянуть.html>гря́нуть</a> (7345)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*grędnǫti</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грянуть.html>гря́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grjánutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to break out, to burst out, to burst forth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гром.html>гром</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:грянуть.html>гря́нул</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">grom <b>grjánul</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there was a clap/crash/peal of thunder</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:грянуть.html>гря́нул</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выстрел.html>вы́стрел</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>grjánul</b> výstrel</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a shot rang out</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(song, orchestra)</i> to strike up</li></ol>

***грясти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:грясти.html>грясти́</a> (22512)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">грѧсти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gręsti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gręsti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*GʰrHdʰ-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gradior</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">गृध्यति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gṛdhyati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to endeavour to gain, to covet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌲𐍂𐌹𐌳</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grid</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">step</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">progress</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">congress</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ingress</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grade</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грясти.html>грясти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grjastí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пригрясти́</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грянуть.html>гря́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come forth</li></ol>

***губа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губа́</a> (456)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gǫba</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губа́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gubá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>гу́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>гу́б</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lip
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губа́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дура.html>ду́ра</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U vas <b>gubá</b> ne dúra.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You have good taste.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> polypore, sponge</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губка.html>гу́бка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gúbka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губка.html>гу́бка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gúbka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губной.html>губно́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gubnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пригубить.html>пригу́бить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prigúbitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to taste; to try (more frequently about wines</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губа́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дура.html>ду́ра</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gubá ne dúra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*guba</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, action noun of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gъbnǫti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Alternatively, per Vasmer, from <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губа́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gubá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lip</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, originally "river mouth".
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губа́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gubá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>гу́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>гу́б</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">North Russia</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bay, inlet</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залить.html>зали́в</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zalív</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухта.html>бу́хта</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">búxta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortening of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">губва́хта</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gubváxta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a corruption of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гауптвахта.html>гауптва́хта</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gauptváxta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губа́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gubá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губы́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stockade <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">prison</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> detention in a stockade (as a punishment)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сажать.html>сажа́ть</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:отправлять.html>отправля́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губу́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sažátʹ/otpravljátʹ na <b>gubú</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to confine to stockade</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***губернский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:губернский.html>губе́рнский</a> (12845)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губерния.html>губе́рния</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gubérnija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губернский.html>губе́рнский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gubérnskij</span>)
</p>

***губить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:губить.html>губи́ть</a> (9996)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gubiti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:губить.html>губи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gubítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погубить.html>погуби́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгубить.html>сгуби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wreck, to destroy, to ruin</li>
<li>to kill <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">make useless</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to waste</li></ol>

***гудеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гудеть.html>гуде́ть</a> (3123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a common Slavic root. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">гуді́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hudíty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">гусці́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">huscí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">gódem</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гудеть.html>гуде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gudétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прогудеть.html>прогуде́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загудеть.html>загуде́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to buzz; to drone; to hoot, to honk</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to party, revel</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гудок.html>гудо́к</a> (5553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гудеть.html>гуде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gudétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гудок.html>гудо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gudók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гудок.html>гудка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гудок.html>гудки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гудок.html>гудко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hooter; toot; siren; honk; whistle (ship, train, factory, car, etc.)</li>
<li>gudok <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an ancient Russian musical instrument</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><b>гу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:док.html>до́к</a></b>

***гулливер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гулливер.html>гулливе́р</a> (17500)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the protagonist <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lemuel_Gulliver" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lemuel Gulliver">Lemuel Gulliver</a> of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jonathan_Swift" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jonathan Swift">Jonathan Swift</a>'s novel <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gulliver%27s_Travels" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Gulliver | s Travels">Gulliver's Travels</a></i>, who found himself a relative giant in a land of tiny people.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулливер.html>гулливе́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gullivér</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулливер.html>гулливе́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулливер.html>гулливе́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулливер.html>гулливе́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>very tall person, giant</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гулянье.html>гуля́нье</a> (22320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулянье.html>гуля́нье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">guljánʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулянье.html>гуля́нья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулянье.html>гуля́нья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулянье.html>гуля́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>walk, walking; stroll</li>
<li>revelry, open-air merrymaking, outdoor fete; (<a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a>) festival</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>гу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ля́нь<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>

Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:художественный.html>худо́жественной</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:особенно.html>осо́бенно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поэтический.html>поэти́ческой</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>ре́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:допустимый.html>допусти́ма</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> предл. пад. ед. ч. <i>гуля́ньи</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> словообразования: <a href = vnd.unilang:гуляние.html>гуля́ние</a>.

***гулять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гулять.html>гуля́ть</a> (1699)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">гуля́ць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">huljácʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">гуляти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">huljaty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулять.html>гуля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">guljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погулять.html>погуля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to walk, to go for a walk, to stroll</li>
<li>to have time-off, to have free time</li>
<li>to make merry, to enjoy oneself, to carouse
<ol><li>to party</li></ol></li>
<li>to go with, to go out <i>with someone</i></li></ol>
